)@@G@@E .   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@MCORE*    L,U       A0,BSIZE          . GET BUFFFZ
)@@G@@ER SIZE.    @C@@@@          S,H1      A0,COPIN+2        . SET     @B@@@@GA
)@@G@@          S,H1      A0,COPOUT+2       .   @F@@@@          L         A0,BGB
)@@G@@IGIN          . GET BUFFER ADDR INPUT.    @C@@@@          S         A0,CGC
)@@G@@OPIN+4        . SET     @D@@@@          L         A0,BIGOUT         . SAGD
)@@G@@ME FOR OUT. @B@@@@          S         A0,COPOUT+4       .   @D@@@@      GE
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,BSEC           . SIZE //28     @C@@@@          S,H1    GF
)@@G@@  A0,COPIN+5        . SET     @B@@@@          S,H1      A0,COPOUT+5     GG
)@@G@@  .   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          L         A0,(IN1+4*BSIZE)  . LOAD HIGGH
)@@G@@HEST ADDR +1.     @F@@@@          S         A0,CURDBL         . SET CURRGI
)@@G@@ENT D BANK LIMIT. @F@@@@          ANU,U     A0,FRSTD$         . SET MCORGJ
)@@G@@E TO # BLOCKS     @C@@@@          S         A1,MCDONE         . IN USE. GK
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AN,U      A0,1              . SET TO LAST ADDR REQ.     GL
)@@G@@@E@@@@          ER        MCORE$            . GET IT FROM SYS.    @C@@@@GM
)@@G@@          J         0,X10             . RETURN  @F@@@@.      ROUTINE TO GN
)@@G@@DO MCORE$ FOR MACRO SAMPLE TEXT AND ARG AREA.   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@MMCOR*GO
)@@G@@    . ENTRY FOR MACRO CORE EXP.     @C@@@@          SZ        A1        GP
)@@G@@        . CLEAR.  @E@@@@          L         A0,CURDBL         . GET CURRGQ
)@@G@@ENT POINTER.@D@@@@          DSL       A0,9              . SHIFT RIGHT 9.GR
)@@G@@@D@@@@          A,U       A0,1              . INCR 1 BLOCK. @C@@@@      GS
)@@G@@    LSSL      A0,9              . RESET . @F@@@@          TNZ       A1  GT
)@@G@@              . WAS THERE A REMAINDER.    @F@@@@          J         BOUNGU
)@@G@@D             . NO, MUST REALLY REQ MCORE.@E@@@@          ON        CLRCGV
)@@G@@R             . ONLY IF NEEDED.     @D@@@@          ANU       A0,CURDBL GW
)@@G@@        . GET # WORDS.  @E@@@@          AN,U      A1,1              . LEGX
)@@G@@SS 1 FOR +1 BELOW.@C@@@@          L         R1,A1             . INTO R1.GY
)@@G@@@D@@@@          LXI,U     A1,1              . SET INCR.     @C@@@@      GZ
)@@G@@    LXM       A1,CURDBL         . ADDR.   @B@@@@          A,U       A1,1HA
)@@G@@              . +1@D@@@@          SZ        0,A1              . CLEAR FOHB
)@@G@@R BT. @^@@@@          OFF       .   @E@@@@          S         A0,CURDBL HC
)@@G@@        . SET NEW POINTER.    @D@@_@          AN,U      A0,FRSTD$       HD
)@@G@@  . LESS START.   @D@@_@          S         A0,MCDONE         . MARK DONHE
)@@G@@E.    @B@@@@          ON        CLRCR             .   @D@@@@          L,HF
)@@G@@U       A0,0,A1           . GET ADDR.     @C@@@@          BT        A1,0HG
)@@G@@,*A0          . CLEAR.  @^@@@@          OFF       .   @C@@@@          J HH
)@@G@@        0,X10             . RETURN. @D@@@@BOUND     . ENTRY IF CURBDL SEHI
)@@G@@T ON BLOCK BOUNDARY.    @F@@@@          L         A0,CURDBL         . GEHJ
)@@G@@T CURRENT END OF D BANK.@D@@@@          A,U       A0,MACBS          . ADHK
)@@G@@D INCR.     @D@@@@          S         A0,CURDBL         . SET NEW LIMIT.HL
)@@G@@@D@@@@          ANU,U     A0,FRSTD$         . LESS START.   @F@@@@      HM
)@@G@@    S         A1,MCDONE         . TURN OFF I/O BUFFER EXP.  @F@@@@      HN
)@@G@@    AN,U      A0,1              . SET TO LAST ADDR IN BLK.  @C@@@@      HO
)@@G@@    ER        MCORE$            . DO IT.  @E@@@@          ON        CLRCHP
)@@G@@R             . ONLY IF NEEDED.     @C@@@@          L,U       R1,MACBS  HQ
)@@G@@        . #WORDS. @C@@@@          LXI,U     A0,1              . INCR.   HR
)@@G@@@C@@@@          LXM       A0,CURDBL         . ADDR.   @D@@@@          ANHS
)@@G@@,U      A0,MACBS          . OF START.     @C@@@@          SZ        0,A0HT
)@@G@@              . CLEAR.  @C@@@@          L,U       A1,0,A0           . ADHU
)@@G@@DR.   @C@@@@          BT        A0,0,*A1          . CLEAR.  @^@@@@      HV
)@@G@@    OFF       .   @C@@@@          J         0,X10             . RETURN  HW
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @^@@@@          END       .   ___     MCORE$            . GEHX

)@@G@@@F@@@@POINTS TO BE GRAPHED. X CONTAINS THE HORIZONTAL COORDINATES (THE  UM
)@@G@@@F@@@@ABSCISSA) AND Y THE VERTICAL COORDINATES (THE ORDINATE). X AND Y  UN
)@@G@@@#@@@@MUST BE TYPE REAL.@[@@@@      @E@@@@    N IS THE NUMBER OF POINTS UO
)@@G@@TO BE GRAPHED. N MUST BE TYPE @B@@@@INTEGER WITH A VALUE FROM 1 TO 10000UP
)@@G@@.     @[@@@@      @F@@@@    LX AND LY ARE THE LENGTHS IN INCHES OF THE RUQ
)@@G@@ESPECTIVE COOR-   @F@@@@DINATE AXES. FOR EXAMPLE, IF LX = 8 AND LY = 6, UR
)@@G@@GRAPH WILL MAKE   @F@@@@THE HORIZONTAL AXIS (X-AXIS) 8 INCHES LONG (= 80US
)@@G@@ POSITIONS) AND   @F@@@@THE VERTICAL AXIS (Y-AXIS) 6 INCHES HIGH (= 36 LUT
)@@G@@INES). (THERE ARE @E@@@@10 CHARACTERS PER HORIZONTAL INCH AND 6 LINES PEUU
)@@G@@R VERTICAL  @F@@@@INCH.) LY MUST HAVE A VALUE FROM 1 TO 100; LX FROM 1 TUV
)@@G@@O 11. LX    @A@@@@AND LY MUST BOTH BE OF TYPE INTEGER.@[@@@@      @E@@@@UW
)@@G@@    LIT IS ONE OF FIVE LITERALS WHICH DEFINE THE SCALE TO BE@ @@@@USED. UX
)@@G@@THE FIVE LITERALS ARE:  @[@@@@      @#@@@@        'NORMAL'  @ @@@@      UY
)@@G@@  'DX=DY' OR 'DY=DX'    @#@@@@        'POLAR'   @#@@@@        'USER'    UZ
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @A@@@@    THESE OPTIONS DO THE FOLLOWING: @[@@@@      @B@@@@VA
)@@G@@(1)     CALL CRAPH (X,Y,M,LX,LY,'NORMAL') @[@@@@      @F@@@@    THIS CALVB
)@@G@@L SCALES AND LABELS THE AXES SO THAT THE GRAPH FILLS  @F@@@@THE LX BY LYVC
)@@G@@ BOX AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE. SUPPOSE, FOR EXAMPLE, THAT  @F@@@@THE X COORDIVD
)@@G@@NATES RANGE FROM 0.15 TO 7.61 AND THAT LX = ,. THE    @F@@@@X-AXIS WOULDVE
)@@G@@ THEN BE SCALED AT 1.0 UNITS PER INCH AND LABELLED    @F@@@@FROM 0.0 TO VF
)@@G@@8.0. SUPPOSE ALSO THAT THE Y COORDINATES RANGE FROM   @F@@@@-0.82E-6 TO VG
)@@G@@2.38E-6 AND THAT LY = 7. THE Y-AXIS WOULD THEN BE     @E@@@@SCALED AT 0.VH
)@@G@@5E-6 UNITS PER INCH AND LABELLED FROM -1.0E-6 TO@]@@@@2.5E-6.     @[@@@@VI
)@@G@@      @B@@@@(2)     CALL GRAPH (X,Y,N,LX,LY,'DX=DY')  @B@@@@    OR: CALLVJ
)@@G@@ GRAPH (X,Y,N,LX,LY,'DY=DX')  @[@@@@      @F@@@@    THIS OPTION ALSO SCAVK
)@@G@@LES THE AXES TO FILL THE GRAPH AS MUCH    @E@@@@AS POSSIBLE BUT WITH THEVL
)@@G@@ RESTRICTION THAT THE TWO AXES ARE  @F@@@@SCALED THE SAME, I.E. HAVE THEVM
)@@G@@ SAME NUMBER OF UNITS PER INCH.     @F@@@@THIS INSURES THAT CIRCLES LOOKVN
)@@G@@ LIKE CIRCLES AND NOT LIKE ELLIPSES @[@@@@      @B@@@@(3)     CALL GRAPHVO
)@@G@@ (X,Y,N,LX,LY,'POLAR')  @[@@@@      @F@@@@    THIS OPTION IS THE SAME ASVP
)@@G@@ (2) ABOVE WITH THE ADDED RESTRICT- @F@@@@ION THAT THE ZERO ON EACH AXISVQ
)@@G@@ IS PLACED IN THE CENTER OF THE     @F@@@@AXIS. (IF LX OR LY IS AN ODD NVR
)@@G@@UMBER THE ZERO IS PLACED 1/2 INCH   @A@@@@DOWN FROM THE CENTER OF THE AXVS
)@@G@@IS.)  @[@@@@      @B@@@@(4)     CALL GRAPH (X,Y,N,LX,LY,'USER')   @[@@@@VT
)@@G@@      @F@@@@    WITH THIS CALL THE USER HIMSELF SUPPLIES THE SCALE. HE MVU
)@@G@@UST   @F@@@@THEN PUT THE LOWER LIMIT AND THE NUMBER OF UNITS PER INCH FOVV
)@@G@@R THE @F@@@@X-AXIS IN X(N + 1) AND X(N + 2) RESPECTIVELY. SIMILARLY Y(N VW
)@@G@@+ 1)  @F@@@@AND Y(N + 2) MUST CONTAIN THE LOWER LIMIT AND THE UNITS PER VX
)@@G@@INCH  @F@@@@FOR THE Y-AXIS. X(N + 2) AND Y(N + 2) MUST BE GREATER THAN ZVY
)@@G@@ERO.  @[@@@@      @F@@@@    SUPPOSE, FOR EXAMPLE, THAT X(N + 1) = 0.0, XVZ
)@@G@@(N + 2) = 0.5,    @F@@@@AND LX = 8. THE X-AXIS WILL THEN BE SCALED AT 0.WA
)@@G@@5 UNITS PER INCH, @F@@@@GOING FROM 0.0 TO 4.0. THE SCALING FOR THE Y-AXIWB
)@@G@@S IS SIMILARLY    @B@@@@DEFINED BY Y(N + 1), Y(N + 2), AND LY.    @[@@@@WC

)@@G@@ARDWARE AND FORMAT CHECKING ROUTINE FOR @OUT.  IT IS USED IN THE  @G@@@@KH
)@@G@@SAME MANNER AS @IN, BUT IT DOES NOT DELETE ANY FILES, AND DOES NOT COPY KI
)@@G@@@G@@@@THE TEXT BACK INTO A FILE.  IT READS THE ENTIRE TAPE, THEREBY CHECKJ
)@@G@@KING  @E@@@@FOR PARITY ERRORS, AND ALSO CHECKS THREE IMPORTANT THINGS:  KK
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @G@@@@     1. THAT THE FILE DESCRIBED ON THE TAPE DESCRIBES KL
)@@G@@A FILE WHICH IS   @ @@@@        CURRENTLY CATALOGUED. @G@@@@     2. THATKM
)@@G@@ THE FILE CONFROMS TO @OUT FORMAT, AND CAN BE READ BY @IN.  @H@@@@     3KN
)@@G@@. AND THAT ALL TRACK ADDRESSES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS SET BY THE FILE'S  KO
)@@G@@@B@@@@        GRANULARITY AND MAXIMUM RESERVE.  @[@@@@      @F@@@@FAILURKP
)@@G@@E OF AN @OUT-FORMAT FILE TO MEET EITHER OF THE FIRST OR LAST@H@@@@REQUIRKQ
)@@G@@EMENTS WILL CAUSE THE PROGRAM TO ABORT.  @IOCHK WILL SKIP OVER ANY NON- KR
)@@G@@@E@@@@ @OUT-FORMAT FILES, PUTTING UP CONSOLE MESSAGES AS DOES @IN.@E@@@@KS
)@@G@@HOWEVER, @IOCHK ABORTS IF IT ENCOUNTERS ANY TYPE OF ERROR.  @H@@@@IT SHOKT
)@@G@@ULD BE NOTED THAT @IN AND @IOCHK WILL READ IN THE ENTIRE SET OF TAPES   KU
)@@G@@@G@@@@PRODUCED BY @OUT, AND WILL LEAVE THEM POSITIONED AFTER THE LAST EOKV
)@@G@@F.    @E@@@@THEREFORE, HAVING MANY NON-OUT TYPE FILES ON A SET OF TAPES KW
)@@G@@@#@@@@IS NOT DESIREABLE.@[@@@@      @E@@@@ @IOCHK PRODUCES A PRINTED LISKX
)@@G@@TING OF EACH FILE IT TRIED TO @F@@@@ @ASG,AY  -- AS WITH @OUT AND @IN, TKY
)@@G@@HE PRINTOUT OCCURS BEFORE     @A@@@@ THE FACT TO AID TROUBLE-SHOOTING.  KZ
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @ @@@@          AVAILABLE OPTIONS:  @[@@@@      @H@@@@      LA

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@THE SORT/MERGE LINKAGE IS A SET OF FOUR SUBROUTINES ENMJ
)@@G@@ABLING A FORTRAN  @F@@@@PROGRAM TO INTERFACE WITH THE SYSTEM SORT/MERGE MK
)@@G@@PACKAGE.  FOR MORE@D@@@@INFORMATION, REFER TO THE LONG VERSION OF THIS IML
)@@G@@TEM.  @[@@@@******@[@@@@      @E@@@@   1106/1108 SORT/MERGE PACKAGE -- FMM
)@@G@@ORTRAN SORT LINKAGE     @E@@@@   IMPLEMENTED BY      SYSTEMS DEVELOPMENTMN
)@@G@@ TECHNICAL SUPPORT@D@@@@                                NEW YORK UNIVERSMO
)@@G@@ITY   @[@@@@      @A@@@@    THE CALL TO INITIALIZE IS :     @[@@@@      MP
)@@G@@@C@@@@          CALL SORTIC (RECL,NUMKS,KEYS,NUMREC)  @[@@@@      @C@@@@MQ
)@@G@@    RECL      IS THE RECORD LENGTH IN CHARACTERS@C@@@@    NUMKS     IS TMR
)@@G@@HE NUMBER OF KEYS (10 MAXIMUM)@E@@@@    KEYS      IS THE ADDRESS OF A 4 MS
)@@G@@X N ARRAY CONTAINING    @A@@@@              THE KEYS (N = NUMKS)  @[@@@@MT
)@@G@@      @A@@@@     THE KEY ARRAY IS OF THE FORM : @[@@@@      @E@@@@      MU
)@@G@@   KEY(1,N)  =  THE KEY TYPE  :  'A' = ALPHANUMERIC   @G@@@@            MV
)@@G@@                           'D' = SIGNED DECIMAL FIELDATA    @F@@@@      MW
)@@G@@                                 'B' = UNIVAC FIXED POINT OR@H@@@@      MX
)@@G@@                                        SINGLE-PRECISION FLOATING       MY
)@@G@@@E@@@@                                              POINT NOTATION@H@@@@MZ
)@@G@@                                       'M' = IBM 7090 FIXED POINT BINARYNA
)@@G@@      @G@@@@                                       'U' = UNSIGNED BINARYNB
)@@G@@ NUMBER     @[@@@@      @E@@@@     FOR MORE DETAILS REFER TO THE 1106/11NC
)@@G@@08 SORT/MERGE PRM.@[@@@@      @D@@@@         KEY(2,N)  =  SEQUENCING ('AND
)@@G@@'=ASCENDING ORDER @D@@@@                      THIS KEY, 'D'=DESCENDING ONE
)@@G@@RDER) @D@@@@         KEY(3,N)  =  CHARACTER POSITION WITHIN THE   @D@@@@NF
)@@G@@                      RECORD OF THE START OF THIS KEY @E@@@@         KEYNG
)@@G@@(4,N)  =  THE LENGTH OF THIS KEY IN CHARACTERS  @[@@@@      @F@@@@    NUNH
)@@G@@MREC    IS THE NUMBER OF RECORDS TO BE SORTED, ITS VALUE    @E@@@@      NI
)@@G@@        MAY BE ZERO, IN WHICH CASE IT IS ASSUMED THAT @C@@@@            NJ
)@@G@@  10,000 RECORDS WILL BE INPUT.     @[@@@@      @D@@@@    TO SORT ON KEYNK
)@@G@@S OTHER THAN ON CHARACTER (6 BIT)   @F@@@@    BOUNDARIES, THE INITIALIZANL
)@@G@@TION CALL MUST BE TO 'SORTIW', WITH @F@@@@    ALL ARGUMENTS UNCHANGED EXNM
)@@G@@CEPT FOR THE LAST TWO WORDS IN THE  @B@@@@    KEY ARRAY (KEY(3,N) AND KENN
)@@G@@Y(4,N)).    @F@@@@    FOR THIS CALL, THESE CELLS MUST CONTAIN THE FOLLOWNO
)@@G@@ING DATA :  @[@@@@      @F@@@@         KEY(3,N)    BITS 35-18 CONTAIN THNP
)@@G@@E NUMBER OF THE WORD    @E@@@@                     IN WHICH IS FOUND THENQ
)@@G@@ MSB OF THE KEY   @D@@@@                     (WORD NUMBERING STARTS AT 0NR
)@@G@@)     @[@@@@      @G@@@@                     BITS 17-0 CONTAIN THE BIT NNS
)@@G@@UMBER OF THE MSB OF     @F@@@@                     THIS KEY (BIT NUMBERINT
)@@G@@NG GOES FROM 1 TO 35,   @A@@@@                     LEFT TO RIGHT).@[@@@@NU
)@@G@@      @F@@@@         KEY(4,N)    CONTAINS THE NUMBER OF BITS IN THIS KEYNV
)@@G@@ FIELD@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @ @@@@     EXAMPLES OF KEY SETUPS : @[@@@@NW
)@@G@@      @G@@@@       SUPPOSE SORTING IS DESIRED ON TWO ALPHANUMERIC KEYS, NX
)@@G@@AND ONE     @F@@@@       KEY OF SIGNED DECIMAL FIELDATA.  THE ALPHANUMERNY
)@@G@@IC KEYS ARE @F@@@@       AT (IN ORDER OF SIGNIFICANCE) CHARACTER POSITIONZ
)@@G@@NS 3 AND 25 @F@@@@       THE FIRST KEY IS 12 CHARACTERS IN LENGTH, AND TOA
)@@G@@HE SECOND IS@F@@@@       40 CHARACTERS LONG.  YOU FORESEE NO MORE THAN 5OB
)@@G@@000 RECORDS,@F@@@@       EACH RECORD 26 WORDS LONG.  THE DECIMAL FIELDATOC
)@@G@@A KEY IS    @F@@@@       AT CHARACTER POSITION 78, AND IS 6 CHARACTERS IOD
)@@G@@N LENGTH    @F@@@@       (COUNTING THE SIGN CHARACTER --  '-' OR '+'   'OE
)@@G@@ ' = '+')   @F@@@@      < KEYS 1 AND 3 ABOVE ARE ASCENDING, KEY 2 IS DESOF
)@@G@@CENDING >   @[@@@@      @G@@@@          THE FOLLOWING IS A POSSIBLE FORTOG
)@@G@@RAN SETUP USING THE ABOVE     @ @@@@            SPECIFICATIONS :  @[@@@@OH
)@@G@@      @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@            OI
)@@G@@   .  @G@@@@         DIMENSION KEY(4,3)/'A','A',3,12,'A','D',25,40,'D','OJ
)@@G@@A',78,6/    @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@      OK
)@@G@@         .  @B@@@@         CALL SORTIC (26*6,3,KEY,5000)    @#@@@@      OL
)@@G@@         .  @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@               .  @F@@@@    SUOM
)@@G@@PPOSE NOW THAT AN APPLICATION REQUIRES SORTING ON AN ARRAY  @G@@@@    OFON
)@@G@@ 2000 FLOATING POINT (BINARY) WORDS, AND THE KEY IS TO BE THE     @F@@@@OO
)@@G@@    MANTISSA OF EACH WORD.  THERE IS ONLY ONE KEY, AND IT IS IN   @^@@@@OP
)@@G@@    DESCENDING ORDER.   @[@@@@      @B@@@@       THE FOLLOWING SETUP IS OQ
)@@G@@AN EXAMPLE :@[@@@@      @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@               .  OR

)@@G@@               .  @#@@@@               .  @#@@@@               .  @E@@@@OW

)@@G@@@[@@@@ABSAD @[@@@@      @F@@@@THE ABSAD COMMAND MAY BE USED TO DETERMINESK
)@@G@@ THE VALUE ASSIGNED BY  @F@@@@THE COLLECTOR TO A PARTICULAR EXTERNALLY DSL
)@@G@@EFINED SYMBOL.  ONLY    @F@@@@REFERENCED SYMBOLS DEFINED BY NON-RLIB$ ROSM
)@@G@@UTINES MAY BE LOOKED UP @F@@@@UNLESS THE COLLECTION SOURCE LANGUAGE INCLSN
)@@G@@UDED A 'TYPE EXTDIAG'   @E@@@@STATEMENT, IN WHICH CASE ALL SYMBOLS MAY BSO
)@@G@@E LOOKED UP.  THE @F@@@@COMMAND FORMAT IS 'ABSAD <SYMBOL>*' WHERE THE TRSP
)@@G@@AILING ASTERISK   @F@@@@INDICATES THAT AN EXTERNAL SYMBOL IS MEANT.  FORSQ
)@@G@@ EXAMPLE, 'ABSAD  @F@@@@SNOOPY*' WOULD PRINT THE ADDRESS OF SNOOPY'S ENTSR
)@@G@@RY POINT 'SNOOPY'.@[@@@@      @[@@@@ALTPRT@[@@@@      @F@@@@THE ALTPRT CSS
)@@G@@OMMAND GIVES THE USER CONTROL OVER THE DISPOSITION OF @F@@@@HIS ALTERNATST
)@@G@@E PRINT FILES.  IN GENERAL, WHEN THE ALTPRT COMMAND IS@F@@@@GIVEN, AND ASU
)@@G@@N ALTERNATE FILE IS IN USE, THE CURRENT ALTERNATE FILE@F@@@@WILL BE @BRKSV
)@@G@@PT'ED.  THIS ACTION MAY BE SUPPRESSED BY EMPLOYING AN @F@@@@ASTERISK (*)SW
)@@G@@ AS THE TRAILING DELIMITER FOR THE PARAMETER:  E.G.,  @F@@@@EITHER 'ALTPSX

)@@G@@ THE 'TYPE' ASSEMBLER DIRECTIVE ALLOWS THE PROGRAMMER TO SPECIFY WHETHERDX
)@@G@@@G@@@@ AN ELEMENT IS SENSITIVE TO THE SETTING OF DESIGNATOR D20 IN THE PDY
)@@G@@RO-   @G@@@@ CESSOR STATE REGISTER (ARITHMETIC EXCEPTION INTERRUPT DESIGDZ
)@@G@@NATOR) AND  @C@@@@ IF SO, WHICH SETTING THE ELEMENT REQUIRES.     @[@@@@EA
)@@G@@      @F@@@@ THE REQUIRED SETTING FOR AN ABSOLUTE ELEMENT IS DETERMINED EB
)@@G@@BY THE@G@@@@ COLLECTOR ACCORDING TO THE SETTINGS OF THE RB ELEMENTS BEINEC
)@@G@@G COLLECTED,@F@@@@ A SYSTEM GENERATION PARAMETER, AND THE TYPE COLLECTORED
)@@G@@ DIRECTIVE. @[@@@@      @C@@@@ THE TYPE DIRECTIVE HAS THE FOLLOWING FORMEE
)@@G@@AT:   @[@@@@      @ @@@@                   TYPE   E   @[@@@@      @F@@@@EF
)@@G@@      WHERE E IS AN EXPRESSION WITH A VALUE OF THREE OR LESS.  THE@D@@@@EG
)@@G@@      INTERPRETATION OF THIS VALUE IS AS FOLLOWS:     @[@@@@      @F@@@@EH
)@@G@@         E = 0     SENSITIVITY UNKNOWN.  D20 IS SET ACCORDING TO A@G@@@@EI
)@@G@@                   SYSTEM GENERATION PARAMETER.  THIS IS THE 'MODE'     EJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@                   THAT IS ASSUMED IF NO TYPE DIRECTIVE IS USED.  EK
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @G@@@@         E = 1     ARITHMETIC FAULT COMPATIBILITY MODEEL
)@@G@@.  D20 = 1 IS     @G@@@@                   REQUIRED.  FLOATING POINT ARIEM
)@@G@@THMETIC FAULTS CAUSE    @F@@@@                   AN INTERRUPT.  THIS IS EN
)@@G@@COMPATIBLE WITH THE 1108@ @@@@                   PROCESSOR. @[@@@@      EO
)@@G@@@G@@@@         E = 2     ARITHMETIC FAULT NON-INTERRUPT MODE.  D20 = 0 IEP
)@@G@@S     @F@@@@                   REQUIRED.  FLOATING POINT ARITHMETIC FAULEQ
)@@G@@TS ARE@F@@@@                   INDICATED BY SETTING DESIGNATORS D21, D22ER
)@@G@@ AND  @G@@@@                   D23.  THERE ARE SIX CONDITIONAL JUMP INSTES
)@@G@@RUCTIONS    @G@@@@                   ON THE 1110 WHICH TEST THESE DESIGNET
)@@G@@ATOR SETTINGS.    @[@@@@      @G@@@@         E = 3     INSENSITIVE.  D20EU
)@@G@@ IS SET BY THE COLLECTOR ACCORD-    @F@@@@                   ING TO THE EV
)@@G@@SENSITIVITY OF THE OTHER RB ELEMENTS@E@@@@                   AND/OR A SYEW
)@@G@@STEM GENERATION PARAMETER.    @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @A@@@@EX
)@@G@@ CHANGE IN EXPRESSION EVALUATION    @[@@@@      @G@@@@ A CHANGE IN LEVELEY
)@@G@@ 12B ASSEMBLER CAUSES SOME EXPRESSIONS TO RETAIN THEIR@G@@@@ 'FORM' AND EZ
)@@G@@'RELOCATION' PROPERTIES WHICH PREVIOUSLY LOST THEM.  THE    @G@@@@ TYPE FA
)@@G@@OF EXPRESSION AFFECTED MOST IS ONE CONTAINIING A FORMED VALUE     @E@@@@FB
)@@G@@ (SUCH AS A LINE-ITEM OR EQUF VALUE) WITHIN PARENTHESIS.    @[@@@@      FC
)@@G@@@ @@@@      LINE A       +(LABEL,0) @ @@@@      LINE B       +(J   TAG) FD
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @G@@@@ PREVIOUSLY, EACH OF THESE LINE-ITEMS WAS GIVEN WHOLE FE
)@@G@@WORD FORM AND RE- @F@@@@ LOCATION (BITS 35 - 0) BY THE ASSEMBLER.  IN LEFF
)@@G@@VEL 12B, THEY EACH@G@@@@ RETAIN THE FORM AND RELOCATION PROPERTIES OF THFG
)@@G@@E EXPRESSION WITHIN THE @G@@@@ PARENTHESIS.  LINE A HAS A FORM OF 18,18 FH
)@@G@@AND IS RELOCATABLE IN BITS    @G@@@@ 35 - 18.  LINE B HAS AN INSTRUCTIONFI
)@@G@@ FORM OF 6,4,4,4,2,16 AND IS RE-    @G@@@@ LOCATABLE IN BITS 15 - 0.  THFJ
)@@G@@IS CHANGE CAN CAUSE AN EXPRESSION WHICH   @G@@@@ CONTAINS A POOR USE OF FK
)@@G@@AN EQUF TO ACT QUITE DIFFERENT IN LEVEL 12B.    @F@@@@ THE FOLLOWING EXAFL
)@@G@@MPLE ILLUSTRATES THIS AND ONE WAY TO AVOID IT.  @[@@@@      @[@@@@      FM
)@@G@@@G@@@@ CODE GEN'D BY 12B    CODE GEN'D BEFORE 12B     ASSEMBLY INSTRUCTIFN
)@@G@@ON    @G@@@@ -----------------    ---------------------     ------------FO
)@@G@@--------    @[@@@@      @F@@@@00 01 00 01 0 000001             -        FP
)@@G@@  DOG  EQUF   1,X1,H2   @[@@@@      @G@@@@77 17 17 17 3 177776   10 00 0FQ
)@@G@@2 00 0 177776  LA A2,TAG-(DOG**0177777)   @[@@@@      @G@@@@10 00 02 00 FR
)@@G@@0 177776   10 00 02 00 0 177776  LA A2,TAG-(0,DOG**0177776) @[@@@@      FS
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @A@@@@ LOCATION COUNTER REFERENCE '&FT
)@@G@@'     @[@@@@      @G@@@@ THE AMPERSAND '&' IS DEFINED AS THE NUMBER OF TFU
)@@G@@HE CURRENT LOCATION     @G@@@@ COUNTER IN USE.  THIS IS DIFFERENT THAN TFV
)@@G@@HE DOLLAR-SIGN '$' WHICH IS   @E@@@@ DEFINED AS THE P VALUE OF THE CURREFW
)@@G@@NT LOCATION COUNTER.    @[@@@@      @#@@@@      EXAMPLE 1:  @^@@@@      FX
)@@G@@             $(6) @B@@@@                   A         EQU  &+1     @[@@@@FY
)@@G@@      @G@@@@ IN THE ABOVE EXAMPLE A WILL HAVE A VALUE OF 7.  ONE USE OF FZ
)@@G@@THE & IS IN @C@@@@ PROC'S WHERE THE LOCATION COUNTER IS NOT KNOWN.@[@@@@GA
)@@G@@      @#@@@@      EXAMPLE 2:  @ @@@@                   A*     PROC@F@@@@GB
)@@G@@                   F      EQU    &         . SAVE LOCATION COUNTER@A@@@@GC
)@@G@@                   $(6)   + DATA    @A@@@@                          + DAGD
)@@G@@TA 1  @G@@@@                   $(F)                    . RESTORE LOCATIOGE
)@@G@@N COUNTER   @ @@@@                          END @[@@@@      @[@@@@      GF
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @B@@@@      ADDITIONAL INFORMATION ON ID LINE   @[@@@@      GG
)@@G@@@H@@@@ TWO ADDITIONS HAVE BEEN MADE TO THE ASSEMBLER ID LINE.  THE NEW FGH
)@@G@@ORMAT IS:   @[@@@@      @D@@@@           'ASM12F*R68-6 MO/DD - HH:MN - (GI
)@@G@@OLD,NEW)'   @[@@@@      @G@@@@ ONE ADDITION IS THE ASTERISK (*) FOLLOWINGJ
)@@G@@G THE ASSEMBLER LEVEL FIELD   @G@@@@ INDICATING THAT THIS IS THE COLLECTGK
)@@G@@ION FOR USE WITH THE 1110 EXEC.     @F@@@@ THIS CHARACTER IS A BLANK FORGL
)@@G@@ THE NON-1110 COLLECTION.  THE OTHER@G@@@@ ADDITION IS THE FIELD FOLLOWIGM
)@@G@@NG THIS BLANK OR ASTERISK WHICH SPECIFIES @F@@@@ THE LEVEL OF THE RLIBS GN
)@@G@@WITH WHICH THE ASSEMBLER IS COLLECTED.    @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@GO
)@@G@@*****^@C@@@@DETAILS OF THE CHANGES MADE IN LEVEL 12B FOLLOW:@[@@@@      GP
)@@G@@@G@@@@ASM12B IS REENTRANT.  CODE OPTIMIZATIONS HAVE RESULTED IN INCREASEGQ
)@@G@@S     @B@@@@IN THROUGHPUT OF UP TO 40% OVER LEVEL 11F.@E@@@@THE FOLLOWINGR
)@@G@@G ADDITIONAL CHANGES HAVE BEEN MADE BY UNIVAC:  @[@@@@      @F@@@@1. THEGS
)@@G@@ D-BANK TABLES, NAMELY, THE ITEM TABLE AND PROCEDURE SAMPLE @E@@@@   TABGT
)@@G@@LE, HAVE BEEN REDUCED IN SIZE BY ABOUT 10K.  THERE    @D@@@@   ALSO IS AGU
)@@G@@ CHANGE IN THE INTERPRETATION OF THE CORE @C@@@@   EXPANSION OPTIONS (R,GV
)@@G@@ M, AND Z) AS FOLLOWS:  @[@@@@      @B@@@@          OPTION         INTERGW

)@@G@@@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @^@@@@  1.   INTRODUCTION     @[@@@@      @[@@@@LJ
)@@G@@      @E@@@@    THE CONVERSATIONAL POST MORTEM DUMP (CPMD) PROCESSOR IS LK
)@@G@@@F@@@@ DESIGNED TO AID THE TERMINAL USER IN DETECTING THE CAUSES OF     LL
)@@G@@@F@@@@ PROGRAM FAILURE.  WHENEVER A PROGRAM TERMINATES, A COPY OF IT IS LM
)@@G@@@G@@@@ DUMPED BY THE EXEC 8 SYSTEM TO A FILE FOR POSSIBLE POSTPROCESSINGLN
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@ CPMD IS A PROGRAM WHICH ENABLES THE TERMINAL USER TO SELECTLO
)@@G@@IVELY @F@@@@ EXAMINE THIS DUMP IN AN INTERACTIVE FASHION.  REGISTER DUMPLP
)@@G@@S AND @F@@@@ DUMPS IN SPECIFIED FORMATS (SUCH AS INTEGER OR INSTRUCTION)LQ
)@@G@@ ARE  @]@@@@ ALLOWED.   @[@@@@      @F@@@@     CPMD ALWAYS LOOKS AT THE LR
)@@G@@CURRENT CONTENTS OF THE DUMP FILE   @F@@@@ (WHOSE NAME IS DIAG$).  THUS LS
)@@G@@TO INITIATE EXAMINATION OF THE DUMP,@F@@@@ ONE TYPES      @CPMD    .   CLT
)@@G@@PMD WILL RESPOND WITH A SIGNON LINE,@G@@@@ AND LIST THE I-BANK AND D-BANLU
)@@G@@K LIMITS OF THE PROGRAM BEING DUMPED.     @F@@@@ IT THEN SOLICITS A COMMLV
)@@G@@AND BY TYPING  FUNCTION?  ONCE THE INITIAL@F@@@@ COMMAND REQUEST HAS BEELW
)@@G@@N ANSWERED, CPMD WILL ASK FOR FURTHER     @B@@@@ COMMANDS BY SIMPLY TYPILX
)@@G@@NG AN ASTERISK.   @[@@@@      @E@@@@     SEVERAL OF THE CPMD COMMANDS ACLY
)@@G@@CEPT NUMERIC VALUES AS  @F@@@@ PARAMETER INPUT. IF A NUMERIC FIELD CONTALZ
)@@G@@INS A DECIMAL POINT, IT @G@@@@ WILL BE TAKEN AS FLOATING POINT; IF IT HAMA
)@@G@@S A LEADING ZERO, IT WILL     @F@@@@ BE TAKEN AS AN OCTAL NUMBER; OTHERWMB
)@@G@@ISE, THE NUMBER WILL BE INPUT @G@@@@ AS A DECIMAL INTEGER.  CPMD COMMANDMC
)@@G@@S MAY BE ABBREVIATED DOWN TO AS     @F@@@@ FEW LETTERS AS NEEDED TO SPECMD
)@@G@@IFY THE COMMAND UNIQUELY DOWN TO A  @ @@@@ MINIMUM OF ONE CHARACTER.    ME
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @F@@@@       CPMD WAS ORIGINALLY WRITTEN BY B.K. REID OF THEMF
)@@G@@ UOM PHYSICS@F@@@@ DEPT, AND SUBSEQUENTLY MODIFIED BY THE COMPUTER SCIENMG
)@@G@@CE CENTER   @F@@@@ SYSTEM'S STAFF.  IT WAS REWRITTEN BY BEN CRANSTON TO MH

)@@G@@E THE MAJOR DIFFERENCES:@[@@@@      @F@@@@   1. ALL FIELDS WHICH ARE SPEMT
)@@G@@CIFIED AS OCTAL MUST BE INPUT WITH A@F@@@@ LEADING ZERO (0).  IF NO LEADMU

)@@G@@MAL.  THE OLD CPMD WAS DIFFICULT TO @F@@@@ UNDERSTAND AS CERTAIN FIELDS MW
)@@G@@WERE ASSUMED OCTAL AND OTHERS WERE  @G@@@@ ASSUMED DECIMAL.  WE FEEL THAMX
)@@G@@T AN UNAMBIGUOUS CONVENTION IS EASIER     @A@@@@ TO COMPREHEND AND USE. MY
)@@G@@ EXAMPLE :  @[@@@@      @^@@@@          ALPHA 1000,5  @#@@@@           BMZ
)@@G@@ECOMES@^@@@@          ALPHA 01000,5 @[@@@@      @F@@@@   2. MULTIPLY SUBNA

)@@G@@S PLANNED.  EXAMPLE :   @[@@@@      @^@@@@          DP A(1,2,4),5 @[@@@@NG
)@@G@@      @F@@@@   3. ANY ADDRESS MAY BE SPECIFIED AS <OFFSET>/<LCTR>/<ELEMENH
)@@G@@NT>.  @F@@@@ IF <ELEMENT> IS NOT SPECIFIED THE CURRENT DECK (IF ANY) IS NI

)@@G@@@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @F@@@@   5. IF A 'DUMPING' COMMAND INR

)@@G@@ATION @^@@@@----------------------- @[@@@@      @F@@@@     THE FOLLOWINGYO
)@@G@@ IS A BRIEF DISCUSSION OF THE OVERALL PHILOSOPHY@B@@@@AND OPERATING PRINYP
)@@G@@CIPLES OF THE DOWNDATER.@[@@@@      @F@@@@     IN OPERATION, THE DOWNDATYQ
)@@G@@ER READS THE TWO INPUT ELEMENTS,    @F@@@@COPYING THEM TO TWO INTERNAL SYR
)@@G@@CRATCH FILES. THIS IS NECESSARY     @E@@@@BECAUSE THE DOWNDATER EMPLOYS YS
)@@G@@A PAGED INTERNAL SCRATCH PAD, @F@@@@KEEPING ONLY A PART OF EACH ELEMENT'YT
)@@G@@S TEXT IN CORE AT ANY TIME.   @F@@@@THE TWO FILES CALLED SWAP$FILE1 AND YU
)@@G@@SWAP$FILE2 ARE DYNAMICALLY    @F@@@@ASSIGNED WITH NO INITIAL RESERVE, ANYV
)@@G@@D A MAXIMUM OF 3000 TRACKS    @E@@@@EACH.  THE NUMBER OF IMAGES KEPT IN YW
)@@G@@CORE AT ANY ONE TIME IS @F@@@@DETERMINDE BY THE PARAMETER <NUM> CONTAINEYX
)@@G@@D IN ELEMENT DOWN2. IT  @F@@@@IS PRESENTLY SET AT 1000, MEANING 1000 IMAYY
)@@G@@GES WILL BE KEPT IN CORE@F@@@@FOR EACH ELEMENT.  THIS FIGURE WAS CHOSEN YZ
)@@G@@AS A COMPRIMISE BETWEEN @A@@@@PROGRAM SIZE AND SPEED OF OPERATION.@[@@@@ZA
)@@G@@      @F@@@@     IN THE ACTUAL DOWNDATING PROCESS, SEVERAL OTHER FACTORSZB
)@@G@@ ARE  @F@@@@SET IN THE PROGRAM. ONE, THE LOOK AHEAD FACTOR IS DETERMINEDZC
)@@G@@ BY   @F@@@@THE SIZE OF THE ELEMENT BEING EXAMINED. THIS CALCULATED VALUZD
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@DETERMINES HOW FAR AHEAD THE DOWNDATER WILL LOOK AFTER FINDIZE
)@@G@@NG A  @F@@@@'MATCH' TO BE CERTAIN THAT THE MATCH IS NOT SPURIOUS. WHILE ZF

)@@G@@@F@@@@THE FOLLOWING ENHANCEMENTS HAVE BEEN MADE TO HANDLE PMD IN THE    EG
)@@G@@@#@@@@1100 SERIES EXEC: @[@@@@      @F@@@@ALLOWING CONTROL STATEMENTS TOEH
)@@G@@ INTERVENE BETWEEN PMD REQUESTS     @F@@@@------------------------------EI
)@@G@@-------------------------------     @[@@@@      @H@@@@PREVIOUSLY, PMD REEJ
)@@G@@QUESTS WERE HONORED ONLY IF THE REQUEST WAS ENCOUNTERED     @G@@@@IMMEDIEK
)@@G@@ATELY AFTER THE TERMINATION OF AN @XQT OR PROCESSOR CALL AND ALL  @G@@@@EL
)@@G@@@PMD REQUESTS HAD TO BE GROUPED TOGETHER. THE ONLY CONTROL STATEMENTS   EM
)@@G@@@G@@@@THAT COULD INTERVENE WERE @ADD, @TEST, @SETC AND @JUMP. ALL CONTROEN
)@@G@@L     @F@@@@STATEMENTS ARE NOW ALLOWED BETWEEN THE TERMINATION OF ANY @XEO
)@@G@@QT OR @G@@@@PROCESSOR CALL. ADDITIONALLY, ALL CONTROL STATEMENTS ARE ALLEP
)@@G@@OWED TO     @G@@@@INTERVENE BETWEEN @PMD REQUESTS. IF ANOTHER @XQT OR PREQ
)@@G@@OCESSOR CALL IS   @F@@@@ENCOUNTERED, IT IS HONORED AND DIAG$ IS REWRITTNER
)@@G@@ WHEN THAT @XQT OR@G@@@@PROCESSOR TERMINATES. ALSO NOTE THAT NEW AND EXIES
)@@G@@STING OPTIONS FOR THE   @G@@@@@RUN CARD CAN DIRECT DIAG$ NOT TO BE WRITTET
)@@G@@EN AND THEREFORE 'PMD NOT     @B@@@@ALLOWED' SITUATIONS ARE STILL POSSIBEU
)@@G@@LE.   @[@@@@      @D@@@@ACTIONS FOLLOWING AN @XQT THAT TERMINATE NORMALLEV
)@@G@@Y     @D@@@@--------------------------------------------------    @[@@@@EW
)@@G@@      @F@@@@@PMD REQUESTS ARE HONORED AS DESCRIBED ABOVE WITH THE FOLLOWEX
)@@G@@ING   @#@@@@RESTRICTIONS:     @[@@@@      @F@@@@A.  IF THE 'Y' OPTION ISEY
)@@G@@ NOT SPECIFIED ON THR @RUN CARD, AND THE  @F@@@@    EXECUTE THAT JUST TEEZ
)@@G@@RMINATED WAS A LIB$ PROCESSOR CALL, @PMD'S@F@@@@    ARE NOT ALLOWED UNTIFA
)@@G@@L AFTER THE EXECUTION OF THE NEXT USER    @ @@@@    SUPPLIED ABSOLUTE ELFB
)@@G@@EMENT.@F@@@@B.  @PMD REQUESTS ARE NEVER HONORED IF THE 'N' OPTION IS SPEFC
)@@G@@CIFIED@^@@@@    ON THE @RUN CARD.   @F@@@@C.  @PMD IS NOT CONSIDERED A LFD
)@@G@@IB$ PROCESSOR AND @PMD'S OF THE     @B@@@@    @PMD PROCESSOR WILL NEVER FE
)@@G@@BE TAKEN.   @[@@@@      @D@@@@ACTIONS FOLLOWING AN @XQT THAT TERMINATED FF
)@@G@@IN ERROR    @D@@@@--------------------------------------------------    FG
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @E@@@@THERE ARE NO CHANGES MADE IN THIS AREA. ONLY @PMD CALLFH
)@@G@@S AND @E@@@@CONDITIONAL STATEMENTS(@TEST, @JUMP, @SETC, AND @ADD) WILL  FI
)@@G@@@ @@@@BE PROCESSED AFTER AN ERROR.  @[@@@@      @E@@@@ACTIONS FOLLOWING FJ
)@@G@@AN @XQT THAT TERMINATED IN ABORT MODE     @E@@@@------------------------FK
)@@G@@-------------------------------     @[@@@@      @F@@@@THERE ARE NO CHANGFL
)@@G@@ES IN THIS AREA. THE RUN IS TERMINATED AND @PMD @#@@@@IS NOT ALLOWED.   FM
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @E@@@@ACTIONS WHILE IN DEMAND MODE FOLLOWING AN @XQT TERMINAFN
)@@G@@TION  @E@@@@----------------------------------------------------------  FO
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @F@@@@@PMD'S ARE ALLOWED AS DESCRIBED ABOVE REGARDLESS OF HOFP
)@@G@@W THE @XQT  @]@@@@TERMINATED  @[@@@@      @F@@@@AUTOMATIC @PMD OF LIB$ PFQ
)@@G@@ROCESSORS AND USER PROGRAMS THAT TERMINATE@G@@@@------------------------FR
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------    @#@@@@IN ERROR MODE     FS
)@@G@@@#@@@@-------------     @[@@@@      @G@@@@THE 'W' OPTION HAS BEEN INTRODFT
)@@G@@UCED FOR USE ON THE @RUN CARD. WHEN THE   @G@@@@'W' OPTION IS SPECIFIED FU
)@@G@@AND THE USER IS IN BATCH MODE, IT DIRECTS THE   @G@@@@EXEC TO WRITE ALL FV
)@@G@@USER PROGRAMS AND LIB$ PROCESSORS TO DIAG$ ONLY WHEN  @G@@@@THE PROGRAM FW
)@@G@@OR PROCESSOR TERMINATES IN ERROR. IN ADDITION, THE @PMD     @H@@@@PROCESFX
)@@G@@SOR IS AUTOMATICALLY LOADED TO PRINT A @PMD OF THE ERRORING PROGRAM     FY
)@@G@@@G@@@@OR PROCESSOR. IF THE USER PROGRAM OR LIB$ PROCESSOR ABORT TERMINATFZ
)@@G@@ES    @G@@@@OR TERMINATES NORMALLY, AND THE 'W' OPTION WAS SPECIFIED, THGA
)@@G@@E PROGRAM   @G@@@@OR PROCESSOR IS NOT WRITTEN TO DIAG$ AND @PMD'S ARE NOGB
)@@G@@T ALLOWED. IF THE @G@@@@'W' OPTION IS SPECIFIED ON THE @RUN CARD IN DEMAGC
)@@G@@ND MODE, IT IS IGNORED. @[@@@@      @G@@@@THE USE OF THE 'Y' AND 'N' OPTGD
)@@G@@IONS ON THE @RUN CARD HAS NOT CHANGED.    @[@@@@      @G@@@@THE 'W' OPTIGE
)@@G@@ON DOES NOT OVERRIDE THE 'N' OPTION. IF BOTH OPTIONS ARE    @B@@@@SPECIFGF
)@@G@@IED, THE 'W' OPTION IS IGNORED.     @[@@@@      @G@@@@THE THE 'W' OPTIONGG
)@@G@@ IS SPECIFIED WITH 'Y' OPTION ON THE @RUN CARD, ALL   @G@@@@LIB$ PROCESSGH
)@@G@@ORS AND ALL USER PROGRAMS ARE WRITTEN TO DIAG$. IN ADDITION,@F@@@@AN AUTGI
)@@G@@OMATIC @PMD OF ALL ERRORING PROGRAMS AND LIB$ PROCESSORS IS @]@@@@RECEIVGJ
)@@G@@ED.   @[@@@@      @G@@@@ALL AUTOMATIC @PMD'S ARE TAKEN WITH THE 'P' AND GK
)@@G@@'L' OPTIONS SPECIFIED.  @[@@@@      @F@@@@AN AUTOMATIC @PMD OF THE @PMD GL

)@@G@@E FOUND TO FIT IN A     @F@@@@CERTAIN CATEGORY OR HAVE CERTAIN ATTRIBUTEFF

)@@G@@CH IT CAN LIST.   @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @#@@@@PROCESSOR CALL    @#@@@@FJ
